BFS from the entry-point function to compute the full reachable set\n    12→    5. Report any manifest target NOT in the reachable set as a GAP\n    13→\n    14→Cross-module import resolution:\n    15→    - ``from X import Y`` is resolved by converting the dotted module path\n    16→      to a filesystem path relative to ``source_root``\n    17→    - Relative imports (``from . import X``, ``from ..sub import Y``) are\n    18→      resolved against the importing module's package directory\n    19→    - Missing modules are recorded but do not crash the analyzer\n    20→\n    21→Lazy import handling:\n    22→    - Imports inside ``ast.FunctionDef`` / ``ast.AsyncFunctionDef`` bodies\n    23→      ARE included in the call graph for that function, because these are\n    24→      real runtime paths (e.g. circular-dependency avoidance patterns)\n    25→\n    26→Documented limitations (NFR-6):\n    27→    1. **Dynamic dispatch false negatives** — calls via ``getattr()``,\n    28→       ``**kwargs`` delegation, string-based dispatch (e.g. registry\n    29→       lookups like ``REGISTRY[key]()``) are invisible to static AST\n    30→       analysis. The analyzer will report these targets as UNREACHABLE\n    31→       even if they execute at runtime. Mitigation: use the wiring\n    32→       manifest ``required_reachable`` entries to declare expectations\n    33→       and accept known false negatives via allowlists.\n    34→    2. **TYPE_CHECKING exclusions** — imports guarded by\n    35→       ``if TYPE_CHECKING:`` blocks are excluded from the call graph\n    36→       because they never execute at runtime.\n    37→    3. **Function-scope lazy imports included** — imports nested inside\n    38→       function bodies (e.g. ``def foo(): from bar import baz``) are\n    39→       treated as reachable from that function. 202→\n   203→\n   204→class _CallGraphVisitor(ast.NodeVisitor):\n   205→    \"\"\"Build a per-module call graph from AST.\n   206→\n   207→    For each function/method definition, collects:\n   208→    - Names called via ``ast.Call`` nodes\n   209→    - Names imported at function scope (lazy imports)\n   210→    - Cross-module import mappings at module level and function level\n   211→    \"\"\"\n     self.call_graph: dict[str, set[str]] = {}\n   217→        # local_name -> fully-qualified imported name\n   218→        self.import_map: dict[str, str] = {}\n   219→        # Track current 223→\n   224→    def visit_If(self, node: ast.If) -> None:\n   225→        \"\"\"Detect ``if TYPE_CHECKING:`` blocks and skip their body.\"\"\"\n   226→        if self._is_type_checking_guard(node.test):\n   227→            # Skip the body — these imports don't run at runtime\n   228→            # But still visit orelse (the else branch runs at runtime)\n   229→            for child in node.orelse:\n   230→                self.visit(child)\n   231→            return\n   232→        self.generic_visit(node)\n   233→\n   234→    def _is_type_checking_guard(self, test: ast.expr) -> bool:\n   235→        \"\"\"Check if an if-test is ``TYPE_CHECKING`` or ``typing.TYPE_CHECKING``.\"\"\"\n   236→        if isinstance(test, ast.Name) and test.id == \"TYPE_CHECKING\":\n   237→            return True\n   238→        if (\n   239→            isinstance(test, ast.Attribute)\n   240→            and isinstance(test.value, ast.Name)\n   241→            and test.value.id == \"typing\"\n   242→            and test.attr == \"TYPE_CHECKING\"\n   243→        ):\n   244→            return True\n   245→        return False\n   246→\n   247→    def visit_Import(self, node: ast.Import) -> None:\n   248→        \"\"\"Handle ``import X`` and ``import X as Y``.\"\"\"\n   249→        for alias in node.names:\n   250→            local_name = alias.asname or alias.name\n   251→            self.import_map[local_name] = alias.name\n   252→            # If inside a function, record as a callable edge\n   253→            if self._current_function is not None:\n   254→                self.call_graph.setdefault(self._current_function, set()).add(local_name)\n   255→\n   256→    def visit_ImportFrom(self, node: ast.ImportFrom) -> None:\n   257→        \"\"\"Handle ``from X import Y`` and relative imports.\"\"\"\n   258→        if self._in_type_checking:\n   259→            return\n   260→        base_module = node.module or \"\"\n   261→        if node.level > 0:\n   262→            # Relative import — resolve against current module's package\n   263→            base_module =            fqn = f\"{base_module}.{alias.name}\" if base_module else alias.name\n   268→                self.import_map[local_name] = fqn\n   269→                if self._current_function is not None:\n   270→                    self.call_graph.setdefault(self._current_function, set()).add(\n   271→                        local_name\n   272→                    )\n   273→\n   274→    def 277→        # Go up `level` packages (each level = one parent)\n   278→        if level <= len(parts):\n   279→            base = \".\".join(parts[:-level]) if level > 0 else self.module_name\n   280→        else:\n   281→            base = \"\"\n   282→        if module:\n   283→            return f\"{base}.{module}\" if base else module\n   284→        return base\n   285→\n   286→    def      self._visit_function(node)\n   291→\n   292→    def _visit_function(self, node: ast.FunctionDef | ast.AsyncFunctionDef) -> None:\n   293→        \"\"\"Process a function definition: build call edges from its body.\"\"\"\n   294→        fqn = f\"{self.module_name}.{node.name}\"\n   295→        if self._current_function is not None:\n   296→            # Nested function — treat as callable from parent\n   297→            parent = self._current_function\n   298→            self.call_graph.setdefault(parent, set()).add(fqn)\n   299→\n   300→        prev_function = self._current_function\n   301→        self._current_function = fqn\n   302→        self.call_graph.setdefault(fqn, set())\n   303→        self.generic_visit(node)\n   304→        self._current_function = prev_function\n   305→\n   306→    def visit_Call(self, node: ast.Call) -> None:\n   307→        \"\"\"Record function calls.\"\"\"\n   308→        if self._current_function is None:\n   309→            self.generic_visit(node)\n   310→            return\n   311→        name = self._resolve_call_name(node.func)\n   312→        if name:\n   313→            self.call_graph.setdefault(self._current_function, set()).add(name)\n   314→        self.generic_visit(node)\n   315→\n   316→    def _resolve_call_name(self, node: ast.expr) -> str | None:\n   317→        \"\"\"Extract the callable name from a Call node's func attribute.\"\"\"\n   318→        if isinstance(node, ast.Name):\n   319→            return node.id\n   320→        if isinstance(node, ast.Attribute):\n   321→            # e.g. self.method() or module.function()\n   322→            value_name = self._resolve_call_name(node.value)\n   323→            if value_name:\n   324→                return f\"{value_name}.{node.attr}\"\n   325→            return node.attr\n   326→        return None\n   327→\n   328→\n   329→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   330→# Module resolution\n   331→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   332→\n   333→\n   334→def _module_to_path(module: str, source_root: Path) -> Path | None:\n   335→    \"\"\"Convert a dotted module path to a filesystem path.\n   336→\n   337→    Tries both ``module/path.py`` and ``module/path/__init__.py``.\n   338→    Returns None if neither exists.\n   339→    \"\"\"\n   340→    parts = module.split(\".\")\n   341→    # Try as a .py file\n   342→    candidate = source_root / Path(*parts).with_suffix(\".py\")\n   343→    if candidate.is_file():\n   344→        return candidate\n   345→    # Try as a package __init__.py\n   346→    candidate = source_root / Path(*parts) / \"__init__.py\"\n   347→    if candidate.is_file():\n   348→        return candidate\n   349→    return None\n   350→\n   351→\n   352→def _path_to_module(file_path: Path, \"__init__.py\":\n   356→        parts = rel.parent.parts\n   357→    else:\n   358→        parts = (*rel.parent.parts, rel.stem)\n   359→    return \".\".join(parts)\n   360→\n   361→\n   362→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   363→# ReachabilityAnalyzer\n   364→# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------\n   365→\n   366→\n   367→class ReachabilityAnalyzer:\n   368→    \"\"\"AST-based call-chain reachability analyzer.\n   369→\n   370→    Given a wiring manifest declaring entry points and required targets,\n   371→    parses Python source files, builds a cross-module call graph, and\n   372→    uses BFS to determine which targets are statically reachable.\n   373→\n   374→    Args:\n   375→        manifest_path: Path to the wiring manifest YAML file.\n   376→    \"\"\"\n   377→\n   378→    def __init__(self, manifest_path: Path) -> None:\n   379→        self.manifest_path = manifest_path\n ReachabilityAnalyzer:\n    \"\"\"AST-based call-chain reachability analyzer.\n\n    Given a wiring manifest declaring entry points and required targets,\n    parses Python source files, builds a cross-module call graph, and\n    uses BFS to determine which targets are statically reachable.\n\n    Args:\n        manifest_path: Path to the wiring manifest YAML file.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self, manifest_path: Path) -> None:\n        self.manifest_path = manifest_path\n        self.entry_points, self.targets = load_manifest(manifest_path)\n        # Accumulated cross-module call graph: fqn -> set of called fqns\n        self._global_graph: dict[str, set[str]] = {}\n        # Accumulated import maps: module_name -> {local_name: fqn}\n        self._import_maps: dict[str, dict[str, str]] = {}\n        # Modules already parsed (avoid re-parsing)\n        self._parsed_modules: set[str] = set()\n        self._modules_failed: list[str] = []\n\n    def analyze(self, source_root: Path) -> ReachabilityReport:\n        \"\"\"Run reachability analysis from source_root.\n\n        Args:\n            source_root: Root directory containing Python source packages.\n                Module paths from the manifest are resolved relative to this.\n\n        Returns:\n            ReachabilityReport with per-target results and gap list.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Phase 1: Parse entry point modules and follow imports\n        for ep in self.entry_points:\n            self._parse_module_recursive(ep.module, source_root)\n\n        # Phase 2: Resolve local names in call graph to FQNs\n        resolved_graph = self._resolve_graph()\n\n        # Phase 3: BFS for each target\n        report = ReachabilityReport(\n            modules_parsed=len(self._parsed_modules),\n            modules_failed=list(self._modules_failed),\n        )\n\n        for target in self.targets:\n            # Find the entry point's FQN\n            ep_fqn = self._find_entry_fqn(target.from_entry)\n            if ep_fqn is None:\n                result = ReachabilityResult(\n                    target=target.target,\n                    from_entry=target.from_entry,\n                    spec_ref=target.spec_ref,\n                    reachable=False,\n                )\n                report.results.append(result)\n                report.gaps.append(result)\n                continue\n\n            reachable, chain = self._bfs_reachable(\n                resolved_graph, ep_fqn, target.target\n            )\n            result = ReachabilityResult(\n                target=target.target,\n                from_entry=target.from_entry,\n                spec_ref=target.spec_ref,\n                reachable=reachable,\n                chain=chain,\n            )\n            report.results.append(result)\n            if not reachable:\n                report.gaps.append(result)\n\n        report.passed = len(report.gaps) == 0\n        return report\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Internal: recursive module parsing\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _parse_module_recursive(\n        self, module_name: str, source_root: Path, depth: int = 0\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Parse a module and recursively follow its imports.\"\"\"\n        if module_name in self._parsed_modules:\n            return\n        if depth > 50:\n            logger.warning(\"Import depth limit reached for %s\", module_name)\n            return\n\n        self._parsed_modules.add(module_name)\n        file_path = _module_to_path(module_name, source_root)\n        if file_path is None:\n            logger.debug(\"Module not found on disk: %s\", module_name)\n            return\n\n        try:\n            source = file_path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n            tree = ast.parse(source, filename=str(file_path))\n        except (SyntaxError, UnicodeDecodeError) as exc:\n            logger.warning(\"Failed to parse %s: %s\", file_path, exc)\n            self._modules_failed.append(module_name)\n            return\n\n        visitor = _CallGraphVisitor(module_name)\n        visitor.visit(tree)\n\n        # Merge into global graph\n        for func, callees in visitor.call_graph.items():\n            self._global_graph.setdefault(func, set()).update(callees)\n\n        # Store import map for later resolution\n        self._import_maps[module_name] = visitor.import_map\n\n        # Recurse into imported modules (both module-level and function-scope)\n        for fqn in visitor.import_map.values():\n            # Extract the top-level module from FQN\n            imported_module = self._extract_module(fqn, source_root)\n            if imported_module and imported_module not in self._parsed_modules:\n                self._parse_module_recursive(imported_module, source_root, depth + 1)\n\n    def _extract_module(self, fqn: str, source_root: Path) -> str | None:\n        \"\"\"Try progressively shorter prefixes of a FQN to find a module on disk.\"\"\"\n        parts = fqn.split(\".\")\n        # Try longest prefix first (e.g. a.b.c -> a.b.c, a.b, a)\n        for i in range(len(parts), 0, -1):\n            candidate = \".\".join(parts[:i])\n            if _module_to_path(candidate, source_root) is not None:\n                return candidate\n        return None\n\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n    # Internal: resolve local names to FQNs\n    # ------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    def _resolve_graph(self) -> dict[str, set[str]]:\n        \"\"\"Resolve local call names to fully-qualified names using import maps.\n\n        For each function in the global graph, resolves its callees:\n        - If a callee is already an FQN in the graph, keep it\n        - If a callee matches an import map entry, resolve to FQN\n        - If a callee contains a dot (e.g. ``self.method``), attempt\n          attribute-based resolution\n        \"\"\"\n        resolved: dict[str, set[str]] = {}\n\n        for func, callees in self._global_graph.items():\n            # Determine which module this function belongs to\n            func_module = self._func_to_module(func)\n            import_map = self._import_maps.get(func_module, {})\n\n            resolved_callees: set[str] = set()\n            for callee in callees:\n                resolved_name = self._resolve_name(callee, func_module, import_map)\n                resolved_callees.add(resolved_name)\n\n            resolved[func] = resolved_callees\n\n        return resolved\n\n    def _func_to_module(self, fqn: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Extract module name from a function FQN.\n\n        E.g. ``a.b.c.func`` -> tries ``a.b.c``, ``a.b``, ``a`` against\n        parsed modules.\n        \"\"\"\n        parts = fqn.split(\".\")\n        for i in range(len(parts) - 1, 0, -1):\n            candidate = \".\".join(parts[:i])\n            if candidate in self._parsed_modules:\n                return candidate\n        return parts[0] if parts else \"\"\n\n    def _resolve_name(\n        self, name: str, func_module: str, import_map: dict[str, str]\n    ) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Resolve a local name to its best FQN guess.\"\"\"\n        # Direct match in import map\n        if name in import_map:\n            return import_map[name]\n\n        # Dotted name — try resolving the prefix\n        if \".\" in name:\n            prefix, _, rest = name.partition(\".\")\n            if prefix in import_map:\n                return f\"{import_map[prefix]}.{rest}\"\n            # Could be module.func — check if prefix is a known module\n            if prefix in self._parsed_modules:\n                  return fqn\n                # Try without the function being directly in graph\n                # (might be defined but we missed it)\n                return fqn\n        return _bfs_reachable(\n        self,\n        graph: dict[str, set[str]],\n        start: str,\n        target: str,\n    ) -> tuple[bool, list[str]]:\n        \"\"\"BFS from ``start`` to ``target`` in the resolved call graph.\n\n        Returns:\n            Tuple of (is_reachable, call_chain).\n            call_chain is the path from start to target (inclusive), or\n            empty if unreachable.\n        \"\"\"\n        if start == target:\n            return True, [start]\n\n        visited: set[str] = set()\n        # Queue entries: (current_node, path_so_far)\n        queue: deque[tuple[str, list[str]]] = deque()\n        queue.append((start, [start]))\n        visited.add(start)\n\n        while queue:\n            current, path = queue.popleft()\n\n            for neighbor in graph.get(current, set()):\n                if neighbor in visited:\n                    continue\n\n                new_path = [*path, neighbor]\n\n                # Exact match\n                if neighbor == target:\n                    return True, new_path\n\n                # Suffix match: target \"a.b.c.func\" matches neighbor\n                # \"a.b.c.func\" or neighbor ends with the target's\n                # function portion\n                if self._is_target_match(neighbor, target):\n                    return True, new_path\n\n                visited.add(neighbor)\n                queue.append((neighbor, new_path))\n\n        return False, []\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def _is_target_match(candidate: str, target: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if candidate matches the target, allowing suffix matching.\n\n        Handles cases where the resolved name might differ slightly\n        from the manifest target (e.g. different import resolution paths).\n        \"\"\"\n        if candidate == target:\n            return True\n        # Extract function name from target (last component)\n        target_func = target.rsplit(\".\", 1)[-1]\n        candidate_func = candidate.rsplit(\".\", 1)[-1]\n        if target_func != candidate_func:\n            return False\n        # Same function name — check if the module paths overlap\n        # (handles aliased module _write_module(source_root: Path, module_dotted: str, source: str) -> Path:\n    \"\"\"Write a synthetic Python module to ``source_root``.\n\n    Handles both ``a.b.c`` -> ``a/b/c.py`` and package \"__init__.py\"\n        if not init.exists():\n            init.write_text(\"\")\n    file_path.write_text(textwrap.dedent(source))\n    return file_path\n\n\ndef _write_manifest(manifest_path: Path,
